(二)上下學期開設者，須先修過（一），始可修（二）；(一) (二)上下學期皆修畢始承認該科學分。<br/>For subjects of faculty that subdivided into parts to be taken on first (1st) and second (2nd) semester, students must clear the (1st) semester in order to enter the (2nd) semester; moreover, credit points will only be recognized with both semesters completed.</li><li>核心選修科目之課程領域須選修8學分。<br/>Students should obtain 8 credit points from core semester; “Poetry and Assignment” - 4 poetries have to be worked out as per semester. “Ci Poems and Assignment” - 2 ci poems have to be worked out as per semester. “Creative Modern Literature Assignment” – 3 assignments have to be completed as per semester.</li><li>現代詩專題、現代散文專題和現代小說專題三門課，應至少先修一門以下課程:該系列課程的「選讀」、「習作」;或「台灣文學史」、「亞洲華文文學」。<br/>For the 3 courses of Modern Poetry Topic, Modern Prose Topic and Modern Novel Topic, students have to complete at least one of its subdivided subject: the “selected readings”, “assignment” of respective courses; or “History of Taiwanese Literature”, or “Asian Chinese Literature”.</li></ol></td></tr></table>

Topics on Modern Prose and Topics on Modern Novel, students have to complete at least one of its subdivided subject: the “selected readings and writing” of respective courses; or “History of Taiwanese Literature”, or “Asian Chinese Literature”.</li><li>【文獻數位化編輯與應用 】(課號CC174)、【文獻大數據管理與應用】 (課號CC297)、【雲端應用與APP設計】(課號CC391)為本系「數位應用相關課程｣，畢業前須通過至少2門(可至本系或外系修習)。</li></ol><p>Before graduation, students have to pass at least two courses from below digital courses: Literature Digitization and Editing Applications(CC174), Big Data Management and Application(CC297) and Cloud Application Design and APP(CC391). (Student may take 'digital application courses' from another department.) .</p></td></tr></table>

Students must score 60 points or higher in Mandarin Chinese (III) and (IV) before taking Mandarin Chinese (V) and (VI).</p><p>英語檢定English Testing（1）、經典五十Fifty Canonized Books（2）、服務學習Service Learning（1）</p></td></tr><tr><td colspan="2"><p>體育Physical Education（0）</p></td><td colspan="4"><p>體育Physical Education（0）</p></td><td colspan="3"><p>體育Physical Education（0）</p></td><td colspan="3"><p>體育Physical Education（0）</p></td><td colspan="2"></td><td></td><td></td><td colspan="2"></td></tr><tr><td colspan="18"><p>體育除修習大一至大二4個學期外，另需通過「游泳能力檢定」及「心肺適能檢定」等二項檢測，列為畢業門檻。</p><p>Beside taking PE courses for 4 semesters (Year 1 to 2), students must pass both swimming and cardiopulmonary function tests.</p></td></tr><tr><td><p>通識教育科目General Education</p><p>（10）</p></td><td colspan="18"><p>通識課程分為人文藝術、自然科學、社會科學及生命科學四大類。學生須於四大領域中各選修2學分課程，共計8學分。General Education program comprises four categories：Humanities, Natural Science, Social Science and Life Science. (Outside the Department of elective up to recognize the (17) credits, and the cooperation courses with other departments, according to the provisions of the highest recognition of credit)</p></td></tr></table>

Topics on Modern Prose and Topics on Modern Novel, students have to complete at least one of its subdivided subject: the “selected readings and writing” of respective courses; or “History of Taiwanese Literature”, or “Asian Chinese Literature”.</li><li>【文獻數位化編輯與應用 】(課號CC174)、【文獻大數據管理與應用】 (課號CC297)、【雲端應用與APP設計】(課號CC391)為本系「數位應用相關課程｣，畢業前須通過至少2門(可至本系或外系修習)。</li></ol><p>Before graduation, students have to pass at least two courses from below digital courses: Literature Digitization and Editing Applications(CC174), Big Data Management and Application(CC297) and Cloud Application Design and APP(CC391). (Student may take 'digital application courses' from another department.) .</p></td></tr></table>

courses from below digital courses: Literature Digitization and Editing Applications(CC174), Big Data Management and Application(CC297) and Cloud Application Design and APP(CC391).(Student may take (Outside the Department of elective up to recognize the (17) credits, and the cooperation courses with other departments, according to the provisions of the highest recognition of credit)</p></td></tr></table>

For those who would like to registered “Fundamental computer programming”, he/she has to meet the college requirement. (Course Name: Fundamental Computer Programming)</p></td></tr><tr><td colspan="18"><p>外語課程應依「通識外語修課規定」修習，共計10學分。</p><ol><li>「英語（一）」及「英語（二）」為基礎課程，採能力分級上課，共計二學期四學分。</li><li>除了「英語（一）」及「英語（二）」外，應修習主題式英語課程三學期5學分，畢業前需修畢三個不同英語課程，始取得畢業資格。大一英語能力後測TOEIC模擬測驗成績未達350分者，應修習「應試加強班」，修習「應試加強班」期間之期末TOEIC模擬測驗成績未達350分者，則該科成績將「不及格」，並應再次修習「應試加強班」，直到取得TOEIC模擬測驗分數達350分(含)始得修習其他主題式英語課程。</li><li>另開設「英語檢定」計一學期1學分，「英語檢定」之修課限制與注意事項，請參照「英語檢定」修課規定，並由通識教學部公佈後施行。</li></ol><p>外國學生改修華語須經國際語言文化中心審核通過始可改修華語課程10學分，其華語課程10學分應含「華語檢定」1學分，「華語檢定」修課限制與注事意項，請參照「英語檢定」修課規定。</p><p>凡本校大學部外國學生(不含交換生)修習「華語一」或「華語二」任一課程成績未達60分，不得修習「華語三」、「華語四」、「華語五」、「華語六」，若修習「華語三」、「華語四」任一課程成績未達60分，不得修習「華語五」或「華語檢定」。</p><p>The undergraduate students must complete 10 required credits of foreign language courses as follows:</p><ul><li>English (I), (II): 4 credits</li><li>English thematic course: 5 credits </li><li>English Test: 1 credit</li></ul><p>English (I) and (II) are 4 credits elementary courses for the freshmen who are grouped on English competence-based to complete within two semesters.</p><p>English thematic courses are 5-credit of English courses; students are required to obtain </p><p>5 credits through 3 different thematic courses for graduation.</p><p>For the requirements of registering “English Testing”, please refer to "the Regulation for Registering English Test" announced and implemented by the College of General Education.</p><p>Foreign students need approval by ILCC for taking 10 credits of Mandarin Chinese courses as alternative courses of English.</p><p>The undergraduate foreign students, exchange students excluded, must score 60 points or higher to pass Mandarin Chinese (I) and (II) before taking Mandarin Chinese (III), (IV), (V), and (VI). Students must score 60 points or higher in Mandarin Chinese (III) and (IV) before taking Mandarin Chinese (V) and (VI).</p><p>英語檢定English Testing（1）、經典五十Fifty Canonized Books（2）、服務學習Service Learning（1）</p></td></tr><tr><td colspan="2"><p>體育Physical Education（0）</p></td><td colspan="4"><p>體育Physical Education（0）</p></td><td colspan="3"><p>體育Physical Education（0）</p></td><td colspan="3"><p>體育Physical Education（0）</p></td><td colspan="2"></td><td></td><td></td><td colspan="2"></td></tr><tr><td colspan="18"><p>體育除修習大一至大二4個學期外，另需通過「游泳能力檢定」及「心肺適能檢定」等二項檢測，列為畢業門檻。</p><p>Beside taking PE courses for 4 semesters (Year 1 to 2), students must pass both swimming and cardiopulmonary function tests.</p></td></tr><tr><td><p>通識教育科目General Education</p><p>（10）</p></td><td colspan="18"><p>通識課程分為人文藝術、自然科學、社會科學及生命科學四大類。學生須於四大領域中各選修2學分課程，共計8學分。General Education program comprises four categories：Humanities, Natural Science, Social Science and Life Science. Students are required to take a 2-credit course from each category to get 8 credits before graduation.</p><p>通識跨域課程General Education Interdisciplinary Course：此2學分學生可自由於通識講座課程、微課自主學習或在地多元文化課群中選課。惟外籍生與工程學院英語學士班、資訊學院英語學士班、人文社會學院英語學士班、電機通訊學院英語學士班學生仍須於四大領域中選課，依各院修課規定辦理。Students can select the 2 credits from a General Education Lecture course, Micro Credit courses, Self-Study courses, or Local-Multicultural courses. Only foreign students and undergraduates of International Programs in the Colleges of Engineering, Informatics, Humanities and Social Sciences, as well as Electrical and Communication Engineering are required to take a 2-credit course from the four categories according to each college’s policy before graduation.</p></td></tr><tr><td rowspan="4"><p>系必修科目Department 3學分為本系必修「議題導向實作」課程。</li></ol><p>Three credits of Practical Work (CC395) is compulsory of topic-oriented implementation course.</p><ol><li>【文獻數位化編輯與應用 】(課號CC174)、【文獻大數據管理與應用】 Applications(CC174), Big Data Management and Application(CC297) and Cloud Application Design and APP(CC391).</p><ol><li>本系必修課程凡分(一)、(二)上下學期開設者，須先修過（一），且學期成績達40分以上，始可修（二）；(一)、(二)上下學期皆修畢者，始承認該科學分。<br/>For compulsory subjects of faculty that subdivided into parts to be taken on first (1st) and second (2nd) semester, students must clear the (1st) semester with 40 credit points and above in order to enter the (2nd) semester; moreover, credit points will only be recognized with both semesters completed.</li><li>系必修習作課程【詩選及習作】、【詞選及習作】為單班課程，習作課程每學期須制定習作。</li></ol><p>   Compulsory subjects of faculty【Selected Poems with Writing Exercise 】and【Selected Ci with Writing Exercise】are single classes. Assignment needed to be drawn up for each semester.</p><ol><li>本系同學總共必須修滿 130學分方可畢業，包括共同必修及通識課程共31學分、本系必修44學分，其餘選修55學分（外系選修至多承認17學分，與他系合作之學程，依學程規定承認最高學分）。</li></ol><p>Student of Dept. of Ad must take 130 credits in total for graduation,include Required Common Courses and General Education courses (31), Department Compulsory courses (44), and Department Elective courses (55). (Outside the Department of elective up to recognize the (17) credits, and the cooperation courses with other departments, according to the provisions of the highest recognition of credit)</p></td></tr></table>

Topics on Modern Prose and Topics on Modern Novel, students have to complete at least one of its subdivided subject: the “selected readings and writing” of respective courses; or “History of Taiwanese Literature”, or “Asian Chinese Literature”.</li><li>【文獻數位化編輯與應用 】(課號CC174)、【文獻大數據管理與應用】 (課號CC297)、【雲端應用與APP設計】(課號CC391)為本系「數位應用相關課程｣，畢業前須通過至少2門(可至本系或外系修習)。</li></ol><p>Before graduation, students have to pass at least two courses from below digital courses: Literature Digitization and Editing Applications(CC174), Big Data Management and Application(CC297) and Cloud Application Design and APP(CC391). (Student may take 'digital application courses' from another department.) .</p></td></tr></table>

courses from below digital courses: Literature Digitization and Editing Applications(CC174), Big Data Management and Application(CC297) and Cloud Application Design and APP(CC391). (Student may take 'digital application courses' from another department.) .</p></td></tr></table>

will only be recognized with both semesters completed.</li><li>系必修習作課程【詩選及習作】、【詞選及習作】為單班課程，習作課程每學期須制定習作。</li></ol><p>   Compulsory subjects of faculty【Selected Poems with Writing Exercise 】and【Selected Ci with Writing Exercise】are single classes. Assignment needed to be drawn up for each semester.</p><ol><li>本系同學總共必須修滿 130學分方可畢業，包括共同必修及通識課程共31學分、本系必修44學分，其餘選修55學分（外系選修至多承認17學分，與他系合作之學程，依學程規定承認最高學分）。</li></ol><p>Student of Dept. of Ad must take 130 credits in total for graduation,include Required Common Courses and General Education courses (31), Department Compulsory courses (44), and Department Elective courses (55). (Outside the Department of elective up to recognize the (17) credits, and the cooperation courses with other departments, according to the provisions of the highest recognition of credit)</p></td></tr></table>

AA-CP-04-CF02 (1.3 版)／102.04.19 修訂
```

Students must score 60 points or higher in Mandarin Chinese (III) and (IV) before taking Mandarin Chinese (V) and (VI).</p><p>英語檢定English Testing（1）、經典五十Fifty Canonized Books（2）、服務學習Service Learning（1）</p></td></tr><tr><td colspan="2"><p>體育Physical Education（0）</p></td><td colspan="4"><p>體育Physical Education（0）</p></td><td colspan="3"><p>體育Physical Education（0）</p></td><td colspan="3"><p>體育Physical Education（0）</p></td><td colspan="2"></td><td></td><td></td><td colspan="2"></td></tr><tr><td colspan="18"><p>體育除修習大一至大二4個學期外，另需通過「游泳能力檢定」及「心肺適能檢定」等二項檢測，列為畢業門檻。</p><p>Beside taking PE courses for 4 semesters (Year 1 to 2), students must pass both swimming and cardiopulmonary function tests.</p></td></tr><tr><td><p>通識教育科目General Education</p><p>（10）</p></td><td colspan="18"><p>通識課程分為人文藝術、自然科學、社會科學及生命科學四大類。學生須於四大領域中各選修2學分課程，共計8學分。General Education program comprises four categories：Humanities, Natural Science, Social Science and Life Science. Topics on Modern Prose and Topics on Modern Novel, students have to complete at least one of its subdivided subject: the “selected readings and writing” of respective courses; or “History of Taiwanese Literature”, or “Asian Chinese Literature”.</li><li>【文獻數位化編輯與應用 】(課號CC174)、【文獻大數據管理與應用】 (課號CC297)、【雲端應用與APP設計】(課號CC391)為本系「數位應用相關課程｣，畢業前須通過至少2門(可至本系或外系修習)。</li></ol><p>Before graduation, students have to pass at least two courses from below digital courses: Literature Digitization and Editing Applications(CC174), Big Data Management and Application(CC297) and Cloud Application Design and APP(CC391). (Student may take 'digital application courses' from another department.) .</p></td></tr></table>

】(課號CC174)、【文獻大數據管理與應用】 (課號CC297)、【雲端應用與APP設計】(課號CC391)為本系「數位應用相關課程｣，畢業前須通過至少2門(可至本系或外系修習)。</li></ol><p>Before graduation, students have to pass at least two courses from below digital courses: Literature Digitization and Editing Applications(CC174), Big Data Management and Application(CC297) and Cloud Application Design and APP(CC391).(Student may take 'digital application courses' from another department.) .</p></td></tr></table>

**Dept. of Chinese Linguistics & Literature, Yuan Ze University**

**List of Required Courses**

**（111學年度入學新生適用Academic Year 2022）**

Amended by the 8th Academic Affairs Meeting, Academic Year 2023, on May 01, 2024

Students will fail the course if they do not score higher than 350 points in TOEIC Mock Exam by the end of the course, and must repeatedly take the course until they can score higher than 350 points. </li><li>“English Testing” (EL360) for the total 1 credit: For the requirements of registering “English Testing”, please refer to "the Regulation for Registering English Test" announced and implemented by the College of General Education.</li></ol><p>Foreign students need approval by ILCC for taking 10 credits of Mandarin Chinese courses as alternative courses of English.</p><p>The undergraduate foreign students must pass Mandarin Chinese (I) and (II) before taking Mandarin Chinese (III) and (IV). Students must pass Mandarin Chinese (III) and (IV) before taking Mandarin Chinese (V) and Chinese Proficiency Test (EL372).</p><p>英語檢定English Testing（1）、經典五十Fifty Canonized Books（2）、服務學習Service Learning（1）</p></td></tr><tr><td><p>體育Physical Education（0）</p></td><td><p>體育Physical Education（0）</p></td><td><p>興趣選項體育optional physical education（0）</p></td><td><p>興趣選項體育optional physical education（0）</p></td><td></td><td></td><td></td><td></td></tr><tr><td colspan="8"><p>大學部必須修習4學期體育課程；其中2學期為大一體育課程原班級上課，另2學期為興趣選項體育課程。</p><p>The undergraduate students must attend the physical education course for 4 semesters; 2 semesters for the freshman physical education courses, the other two semesters for the optional physical education courses.</p></td></tr><tr><td><p>通識教育科目General Education</p><p>（10）</p></td><td colspan="8"><p>通識課程分為人文藝術、自然科學、社會科學及生命科學四大類。學生須於四大領域中各選修2學分課程，共計8學分。General Education program comprises four categories：Humanities, Natural Science, Social Science and Life Science. regulations.</p><ol><li>通識教育科目學分只採計至多10學分，超修之學分將不列入畢業學分。The maximum credits for general education courses is 10, the exceeding credits will not be counted.</li><li>【實務製作】(課號CC395) 3學分為本系必修「議題導向實作」課程。</li></ol><p>Three credits of Practical Work (CC395) is compulsory of topic-oriented implementation course.</p><ol><li>【畢業製作】課程1學分，上課3小時，列為本系終端學習課程。<br/>[Graduation Work] Categorized as the final learning course of faculty, 3 learning hours for the subject with 1 credit point.</li><li>【文獻數位化編輯與應用 】(課號CC174)、【文獻大數據管理與應用】 (課號CC297)、【雲端應用與APP設計】(課號CC391)為本系「數位應用相關課程｣，畢業前須通過至少2門(可至本系或外系修習)。</li></ol><p>Before graduation, students have to pass at least two courses from below digital courses: Literature Digitization and Editing Applications(CC174), Big Data Management and Application(CC297) and Cloud Application Design and APP(CC391).</p><p> (Student may take 'digital application courses' from another department.) .</p><ol><li>本系課程凡為(一)、(二)/上、下學期開設者，須皆修畢始承認該科學分。<br/>For subjects of faculty that subdivided into parts to be taken on first (1st) and second (2nd) semester, credit points will only be recognized with both semesters completed.</li><li>系必修習作課程【詩選及習作】、【詞選及習作】為單班課程，習作課程每學期須制定習作。</li></ol><p>   Compulsory subjects of faculty【Selected Poems with Writing Exercise 】and【Selected Ci with Writing Exercise】are single classes. Assignment needed to be drawn up for each semester.</p><ol><li>本系同學總共必須修滿 130學分方可畢業，包括共同必修及通識課程共31學分、本系必修44學分，其餘選修55學分（外系選修至多承認17學分，與他系合作之學程，依學程規定承認最高學分）。</li></ol><p>Student of Dept. of Ad must take 130 credits in total for graduation,include Required Common Courses and General Education courses (31), Department Compulsory courses (44), and Department Elective courses (55). (Outside the Department of elective up to recognize the (17) credits, and the cooperation courses with other departments, according to the provisions of the highest recognition of credit)</p><p>9.  為增進學生英文能力，鼓勵選修英語授課課程(含英專班)，其修習之課程科目及學分數之認抵需依學系規定辦理。</p><p>To improve students’ English, we encourage students to take the courses in English (including English Bachelor), which courses and credits waiver and transference should be standardized by each department.</p></td></tr></table>

AA-CP-04-CF02 (1.3 版)／102.04.19 修訂
```

Students must score 60 points or higher in Mandarin Chinese (III) and (IV) before taking Mandarin Chinese (V) and (VI).</p><p>英語檢定English Testing（1）、經典五十Fifty Canonized Books（2）、服務學習Service Learning（1）</p></td></tr><tr><td colspan="2"><p>體育Physical Education（0）</p></td><td colspan="4"><p>體育Physical Education（0）</p></td><td colspan="3"><p>體育Physical Education（0）</p></td><td colspan="3"><p>體育Physical Education（0）</p></td><td colspan="2"></td><td></td><td></td><td colspan="2"></td></tr><tr><td colspan="18"><p>體育除修習大一至大二4個學期外，另需通過「游泳能力檢定」及「心肺適能檢定」等二項檢測，列為畢業門檻。</p><p>Beside taking PE courses for 4 semesters (Year 1 to 2), students must pass both swimming and cardiopulmonary function tests.</p></td></tr><tr><td><p>通識教育科目General Education</p><p>（10）</p></td><td colspan="18"><p>通識課程分為人文藝術、自然科學、社會科學及生命科學四大類。學生須於四大領域中各選修2學分課程，共計8學分。General Education program comprises four categories：Humanities, Natural Science, Social Science and Life Science. Topics on Modern Prose and Topics on Modern Novel, students have to complete at least one of its subdivided subject: the “selected readings and writing” of respective courses; or “History of Taiwanese Literature”, or “Asian Chinese Literature”.</li><li>【文獻數位化編輯與應用 】(課號CC174)、【文獻大數據管理與應用】 (課號CC297)、【雲端應用與APP設計】(課號CC391)為本系「數位應用相關課程｣，畢業前須通過至少2門(可至本系或外系修習)。</li></ol><p>Before graduation, students have to pass at least two courses from below digital courses: Literature Digitization and Editing Applications(CC174), Big Data Management and Application(CC297) and Cloud Application Design and APP(CC391). (Student may take 'digital application courses' from another department.) .</p></td></tr></table>

Literature Digitization and Editing Applications(CC174), Big Data Management and Application(CC297) and Cloud Application Design and APP(CC391).(Student may take 'digital application courses' from another department.) .</p></td></tr></table>

**元智大學中國語文學系必修科目表**

**Dept. of Chinese Linguistics & Literature, Yuan Ze University**

**List of Required Courses**

**（112學年度入學新生適用Academic Year 2023）**

112.04.19 一一一學年度第六次教務會議通過

Passed by the 6th Academic Affairs Meeting, Academic Year 2022, on April 19, 2023

113.05.01 一一二學年度第八次教務會議修訂通過

Amended by the 8th Academic Affairs Meeting, Academic Year 2023, on May 01, 2024

(II) for the total 4 credits: English (I) and (II) are 4 credit elementary courses for the freshmen who are grouped on English competence; to complete within two semesters.</li><li>English thematic course for the total 5 credits: English thematic courses are 5-credit English courses; students are required to obtain 5 credits through 3 different thematic courses for graduation. </li><li>Students who do not reach the 350-point threshold of TOEIC Mock Exam in the end of the freshman year must take “English Testing” (EL260) course. Students will fail the course if they do not score higher than 350 points in TOEIC Mock Exam by the end of the course, and must repeatedly take the course until they can score higher than 350 points. </li><li>“English Testing” (EL360) for the total 1 credit: For the requirements of registering “English Testing”, please refer to "the Regulation for Registering English Test" announced and implemented by the College of General Education.</li></ol><p>Foreign students need approval by ILCC for taking 10 credits of Mandarin Chinese courses as alternative courses of English.</p><p>The undergraduate foreign students must pass Mandarin Chinese (I) and (II) before taking Mandarin Chinese (III) and (IV). Students must pass Mandarin Chinese (III) and (IV) before taking Mandarin Chinese (V) and Chinese Proficiency Test (EL372).</p><p>英語檢定English Testing（1）、經典選讀A Guide to Classics (2)、服務學習Service</p></td></tr><tr><td><p>體育Physical Education（0）</p></td><td><p>體育Physical Education（0）</p></td><td><p>興趣選項體育optional physical education（0）</p></td><td><p>興趣選項體育optional physical education（0）</p></td><td></td><td></td><td></td><td></td></tr><tr><td colspan="8"><p>大學部必須修習4學期體育課程；其中2學期為大一體育課程原班級上課，另2學期為興趣選項體育課程。</p><p>The undergraduate students must attend the physical education course for 4 semesters; 2 semesters for the freshman physical education courses, the other two semesters for the optional physical education courses.</p></td></tr><tr><td><p>通識教育科目</p><p>General Education（10）</p></td><td colspan="8"><p>通識課程分為人文藝術、自然科學、社會科學及生命科學四大類。學生須於四大領域中各選修2學分課程，共計8學分。General Education program comprises four categories：Humanities, Natural Science, Social Science and Life Science. Students are required to take a 2-credit course from each category to get 8 credits before graduation.</p><p>通識跨域課程General Education Interdisciplinary Course：此2學分學生可自由於通識講座課程、微課自主學習或在地多元文化課群中選課。惟外籍生與工程學院英語學士班、資訊學院英語學士班、人文社會學院英語學士班、電機通訊學院英語學士班學生仍須於四大領域中選課，依各院修課規定辦理。Students can select the 2 credits from a General Education Lecture course, Micro Credit courses, Self-Study courses, or Local-Multicultural courses. Only foreign students and undergraduates of International Programs in the Colleges of Engineering, Informatics, Humanities and Social Sciences, as well as Electrical and Communication Engineering are required to take a 2-credit course from the four categories according to each college’s policy before graduation.</p></td></tr><tr><td><p>院必修科目</p><p>College</p><p>Compulsory</p><p>（4）</p></td><td 3學分為本系必修「議題導向實作」課程。</li></ol><p>Three credits of Practical Work (CC395) is compulsory of topic-oriented implementation course.</p><ol><li>【畢業製作】課程1學分，上課3小時，列為本系終端學習課程。<br/>[Graduation Work] Categorized as the final learning course of faculty, 3 learning hours for the subject with 1 credit point.</li><li>【文獻數位化編輯與應用 】(課號CC174)、【文獻大數據管理與應用】 (課號CC297)、【雲端應用與APP設計】(課號CC391)為本系「數位應用相關課程｣，畢業前須通過至少2門(可至本系或外系修習)。</li></ol><p>Before graduation, students have to pass at least two courses from below digital courses: Literature Digitization and Editing Applications(CC174), Big Data Management and Application(CC297) and Cloud Application Design and APP(CC391).</p><p> (Student may take 'digital application courses' from another department.) .</p><ol><li>本系課程凡為(一)、(二)/上、下學期開設者，須皆修畢始承認該科學分。<br/>For subjects of faculty that subdivided into parts to be taken on first (1st) and second (2nd) semester, credit points will only be recognized with both semesters completed.</li><li>系必修習作課程、【詩選及習作】、【詞選及習作】為單班課程，習作課程每學期須制定習作。</li></ol><p>   Compulsory subjects of faculty【Selected Poems with Writing Exercise 】and【Selected Ci with Writing Exercise】are single classes. Assignment needed to be drawn up for each semester.</p><ol><li>本系同學總共必須修滿 130學分方可畢業，包括共同必修及通識課程共27學分、院必修程式語言課程共4學分、本系必修44學分，其餘選修55學分（外系選修至多承認17學分，與他系合作之學程，依學程規定承認最高學分）。</li></ol><p>Student of Dept. of Ad must take 130 credits in total for graduation,include Required Common Courses and General Education courses (27) credits , College Compulsory Courses Fundamental Computer Programming (4) credits, Department Compulsory courses (44) credits, and Department Elective courses (55) credits. (Outside the Department of elective up to recognize the (17) credits, and the cooperation courses with other departments, according to the provisions of the highest recognition of credit)</p><p>9.  為增進學生英文能力，鼓勵選修英語授課課程(含英專班)，其修習之課程科目及學分數之認抵需依學系規定辦理。</p><p>To improve students’ English, we encourage students to take the courses in English (including English Bachelor), which courses and credits waiver and transference should be standardized by each department.</p><p>10. 自106學年度起軍訓課程由必修改為選修，該學分納入當學期修課學分數計算，但不納入畢業總學分計算。</p><p>The military education courses are no longer compulsory starting the 106 academic year. The military education courses will not be accumulated to the graduation requirements, but they can be counted as taken credits for each semester.</p></td></tr></table>

(Course Name: Fundamental Computer Programming)</p></td></tr><tr><td colspan="18"><p>外語課程應依「通識外語修課規定」修習，共計10學分。</p><ol><li>「英語（一）」及「英語（二）」為基礎課程，採能力分級上課，共計二學期四學分。</li><li>除了「英語（一）」及「英語（二）」外，應修習主題式英語課程三學期5學分，畢業前需修畢三個不同英語課程，始取得畢業資格。大一英語能力後測TOEIC模擬測驗成績未達350分者，應修習「應試加強班」，修習「應試加強班」期間之期末TOEIC模擬測驗成績未達350分者，則該科成績將「不及格」，並應再次修習「應試加強班」，直到取得TOEIC模擬測驗分數達350分(含)始得修習其他主題式英語課程。</li><li>另開設「英語檢定」計一學期1學分，「英語檢定」之修課限制與注意事項，請參照「英語檢定」修課規定，並由通識教學部公佈後施行。</li></ol><p>外國學生改修華語須經國際語言文化中心審核通過始可改修華語課程10學分，其華語課程10學分應含「華語檢定」1學分，「華語檢定」修課限制與注事意項，請參照「英語檢定」修課規定。</p><p>凡本校大學部外國學生(不含交換生)修習「華語一」或「華語二」任一課程成績未達60分，不得修習「華語三」、「華語四」、「華語五」、「華語六」，若修習「華語三」、「華語四」任一課程成績未達60分，不得修習「華語五」或「華語檢定」。</p><p>The undergraduate students must complete 10 required credits of foreign language courses as follows:</p><ul><li>English (I), (II): 4 credits</li><li>English thematic course: 5 credits </li><li>English Test: 1 credit</li></ul><p>English (I) and (II) are 4 credits elementary courses for the freshmen who are grouped on English competence-based to complete within two semesters.</p><p>English thematic courses are 5-credit of English courses; students are required to obtain </p><p>5 credits through 3 different thematic courses for graduation.</p><p>For the requirements of registering “English Testing”, please refer to "the Regulation for Registering English Test" announced and implemented by the College of General Education.</p><p>Foreign students need approval by ILCC for taking 10 credits of Mandarin Chinese courses as alternative courses of English.</p><p>The undergraduate foreign students, exchange students excluded, must score 60 points or higher to pass Mandarin Chinese (I) and (II) before taking Mandarin Chinese (III), (IV), (V), and (VI). Students must score 60 points or higher in Mandarin Chinese (III) and (IV) before taking Mandarin Chinese (V) and (VI).</p><p>英語檢定English Testing（1）、經典五十Fifty Canonized Books（2）、服務學習Service Learning（1）</p></td></tr><tr><td colspan="2"><p>體育Physical Education（0）</p></td><td colspan="4"><p>體育Physical Education（0）</p></td><td colspan="3"><p>體育Physical Education（0）</p></td><td colspan="3"><p>體育Physical Education（0）</p></td><td colspan="2"></td><td></td><td></td><td colspan="2"></td></tr><tr><td colspan="18"><p>體育除修習大一至大二4個學期外，另需通過「游泳能力檢定」及「心肺適能檢定」等二項檢測，列為畢業門檻。</p><p>Beside taking PE courses for 4 semesters (Year 1 to 2), students must pass both swimming and cardiopulmonary function tests.</p></td></tr><tr><td><p>通識教育科目General Education</p><p>（10）</p></td><td colspan="18"><p>通識課程分為人文藝術、自然科學、社會科學及生命科學四大類。學生須於四大領域中各選修2學分課程，共計8學分。General Education program comprises four categories：Humanities, Natural Science, Social Science and Life Science. credit points from core elective subjects in respective field of studies.</li><li>現代詩專題、現代散文專題和現代小說專題三門課，應至少先修一門以下課程：該系列課程的「選讀及習作」或「台灣文學史」、「亞洲華文文學」。<br/>For the 3 courses of Topics on Modern Poetry, Topics on Modern Prose and Topics on Modern Novel, students have to complete at least one of its subdivided subject: the “selected readings and writing” of respective courses; or “History of Taiwanese Literature”, or “Asian Chinese Literature”.</li><li>【文獻數位化編輯與應用 】(課號CC174)、【文獻大數據管理與應用】 (課號CC297)、【雲端應用與APP設計】(課號CC391)為本系「數位應用相關課程｣，畢業前須通過至少2門(可至本系或外系修習)。</li></ol><p>Before graduation, students have to pass at least two courses from below digital courses: Literature Digitization and Editing Applications(CC174), Big Data Management and Application(CC297) and Cloud Application Design and APP(CC391). (Student may take 'digital application courses' from another department.) .</p></td></tr></table>

**元智大學中國語文學系必修科目表**

**Dept. of Chinese Linguistics & Literature, Yuan Ze University**

**List of Required Courses**

**（113學年度入學新生適用Academic Year 2024）**

113.05.01 一一二學年度第八次教務會議通過

Passed by the 8th Academic Affairs Meeting, Academic Year 2023, on May 01, 2024

113.06.05 一一二學年度第九次教務會議修訂通過

Amended by the 9th Academic Affairs Meeting, Academic Year 2023, on June 05, 2024

114.04.23 一一三學年度第五次教務會議修訂通過

Amended by the 5th Academic Affairs Meeting, Academic Year 2024, on April 23, 2025

<table><tr><td rowspan="2"><p>學年Academic Year</p><p>學期Semester</p><p>科目Subject</p></td><td colspan="4"><p>第一學年1<sup>st</sup> Academic Year</p></td><td colspan="2"><p>第二學年2<sup>nd</sup> Academic Year</p></td><td colspan="2"><p>第三學年3<sup>rd</sup> Academic Year</p></td><td colspan="2"><p>第四學年4<sup>th</sup> Academic Year</p></td></tr><tr><td><p>上Fall</p></td><td colspan="3"><p>下Spring</p></td><td><p>上Fall</p></td><td><p>下Spring</p></td><td><p>上Fall</p></td><td><p>下Spring</p></td><td><p>上Fall</p></td><td><p>下Spring</p></td></tr><tr><td rowspan="5"><p>共同必修科目Common Compulsory</p><p>（17）</p></td><td><p>中文閱讀、思辨與表達（一） Chinese Reading, Critical Thinking, and Expression （I）</p><p>（2）</p></td><td colspan="3"><p>中文閱讀、思辨與表達（二）Chinese Reading, Critical Thinking, and Expression （II）</p><p>（2）</p></td><td></td><td></td><td></td><td></td><td></td><td></td></tr><tr><td><p>英語（一）</p><p>English （I）</p><p>（2）</p></td><td colspan="3"><p>英語（二）</p><p>English （II）</p><p>（2）</p></td><td></td><td></td><td></td><td></td><td></td><td></td></tr><tr><td colspan="10"><ol><li>外語課程應修習 10 學分。</li><li>「英語（一）」及「英語（二）」為基礎課程，採能力分級上課，共計二學期四學分。</li><li>除了「英語（一）」及「英語（二）」外，畢業前應修畢二個不同主題式英語課程，共計 4 學分。</li><li>大一英語能力後測「TOEIC 模擬測驗」成績未達 350 分者，應修習「應試加強班」（EL260）。修習「應試加強班」期間之期末 TOEIC 模擬測驗成績未達 350 分者，則該科成績將「不及格」，並應再次修習「應試加強班」，直到取得TOEIC模擬測驗分數達 350 分（含）始得修習其他主題式英語課程。</li><li>另開設「英語檢定」（EL160）計一學期2學分，「英語檢定」之修課限制與注意事項，請參照「通識外語『英語檢定』修課規定」，並由通識教學部公佈後施行。</li><li>外國學生改修華語須經國際語言文化中心審核通過始可改修華語課程 10 學分，其華語課程 10 學分應含「華語檢定」2 學分，「華語檢定」修課限制與注意事項，請參照「通識外語『英語檢定』修課規定」及「元智大學外籍生華語學分抵免規定」。</li><li>凡本校大學部外國學生修習「華語（一）」或「華語（二）」任一課程成績未達60分，不得修習「華語（三）」、「華語（四）」。若修習「華語（三）」、「華語（四）」任一課程成績未達60分，不得修習「華語檢定」（EL375）。</li><li>The undergraduate students must complete 10 required credits of foreign language courses.</li><li>English （I） &amp; （II） for the total 4 credits: English （I） and （II） are 4 credits elementary courses for the freshmen who are grouped on English competence; to complete within two semesters.</li><li>English thematic course for the total 4 credits: English thematic courses are 4-credit English courses; students are required to obtain 4 credits through 2 different thematic courses for graduation. </li><li>Students who do not reach the 350-point threshold of TOEIC Mock Exam in the end of the freshman year must take English Testing （EL260） course. Students will fail the course if they do not score higher than 350 points of TOEIC Mock Exam by the end of the course, and must repeatedly take the course until they can score higher than 350 points. </li><li>“English Testing” （EL160） is a 2-credit course: For the requirements of registering “English Testing”, please refer to The Regulation for Registering English Test announced and implemented by the College of General Education.</li><li>Foreign students need approval by ILCC for taking 10 credits of Mandarin Chinese courses as alternative courses of English. The 10 credits in Mandarin Chinese courses must include 2 credits for “Chinese Proficiency Test”. For the specific restrictions and considerations for taking the “Chinese Proficiency Test”, please refer to the 'General Education Foreign Language “English Proficiency Exam” Course Requirements' and 'Yuan Ze University Regulations for Exempting the Mandarin Chinese as a Foreign Language Credit ' for more details.</li><li>The undergraduate foreign students must pass Mandarin Chinese （I） and （II） before taking Mandarin Chinese （III） and （IV）. Students must pass Mandarin Chinese （III） and （IV） before taking 'Chinese Proficiency Test' （EL375）.</li></ol><p> <strong>英語檢定English Testing （2）</strong>、經典選讀A Guide to Classics （2）、服務學習Service Learning （1）</p></td></tr><tr><td colspan="2"><p>體育Physical Education（0）</p></td><td><p>體育Physical Education（0）</p></td><td colspan="2"><p>興趣選項體育optional physical education（0）</p></td><td><p>興趣選項體育optional physical education（0）</p></td><td></td><td></td><td></td><td></td></tr><tr><td colspan="10"><p>大學部必須修習4學期體育課程；其中2學期為大一體育課程原班級上課，另2學期為興趣選項體育課程。</p><p>The undergraduate students must attend the physical education course for 4 semesters; 2 semesters for the freshman physical education courses, the other two semesters for the optional physical education courses.</p></td></tr><tr><td><p>通識教育科目</p><p>General Education（10）</p></td><td colspan="10"><p>通識課程分為人文藝術、自然科學、社會科學及生命科學四大類。學生須於四大領域中各選修2學分課程，共計8學分。General Education program comprises four categories：Humanities, Natural Science, Social Science and Life Science. The military education courses will not be accumulated to the graduation requirements, but they can be counted as taken credits for each semester.</p><p>12. 修習碩士班課程以大三以上學生為限，且不得修習碩士在職專班課程。</p><p>Master's degree courses are limited to students in their third year or above, and students are not allowed to take courses from the Executive Master program.</p></td></tr></table>

(課號CC297)、【雲端應用與APP設計】(課號CC391)為本系「數位應用相關課程｣，畢業前須通過至少2門。</li></ol><p>Before graduation, students have to pass at least two courses from below digital courses: Literature Digitization and Editing Applications(CC174), Big Data Management and Application(CC297) and Cloud Application Design and APP(CC391).</p><ol><li>本系必修課程凡分(一)、(二)上下學期開設者，須先修過（一），且學期成績達40分以上，始可修（二）；(一)、(二)上下學期皆修畢者，始承認該科學分。<br/>For compulsory subjects of faculty that subdivided into parts to be taken on first (1st) and second (2nd) semester, students must clear the (1st) semester with 40 credit points and above in order to enter the (2nd) semester; moreover, credit points will only be recognized with both semesters completed.</li><li>系必修習作課程【詩選及習作】、【詞選及習作】為單班課程，習作課程每學期須制定習作。</li></ol><p>   Compulsory subjects of faculty【Selected Poems with Writing Exercise 】and【Selected Ci with Writing Exercise】are single classes. Assignment needed to be drawn up for each semester.</p><ol><li>本系同學總共必須修滿 130學分方可畢業，包括共同必修及通識課程共31學分、本系必修44學分，其餘選修55學分（外系選修至多承認17學分，與他系合作之學程，依學程規定承認最高學分）。</li></ol><p>Student of Dept. of Ad must take 130 credits in total for graduation,include Required Common Courses and General Education courses (31), Department Compulsory courses (44), and Department Elective courses (55). (Outside the Department of elective up to recognize the (17) credits, and the cooperation courses with other departments, according to the provisions of the highest recognition of credit)</p></td></tr></table>
```

to pass at least two courses from below digital courses: Literature Digitization and Editing Applications(CC174), Big Data Management and Application(CC297) and Cloud Application Design and APP(CC391). (Student may take 'digital application courses' from another department.) .</p></td></tr></table>

**元智大學中國語文學系選修科目表**

**Dept. of Chinese Linguistics & Literature, Yuan Ze University**

**List of Elective Courses**

**（113學年度入學新生適用Academic Year 2024）**

113.05.01 一一二學年度第八次教務會議通過

Passed by the 8th Academic Affairs Meeting, Academic Year 2023, on May 01, 2024

core elective field of "Digital Application " are "Digital Application-related Courses" of our department.Students must pass at least 2 courses before graduation (Students can study in our department or external departments).</p></td></tr></table>

114.04.23 一一三學年度第五次教務會議通過

Passed by the 5th Academic Affairs Meeting, Academic Year 2024, on April 23, 2025

<table><tr><td rowspan="2"><p>學年Academic Year</p><p>學期Semester</p><p>科目Subject</p></td><td colspan="4"><p>第一學年1<sup>st</sup> Academic Year</p></td><td colspan="2"><p>第二學年2<sup>nd</sup> Academic Year</p></td><td colspan="2"><p>第三學年3<sup>rd</sup> Academic Year</p></td><td colspan="2"><p>第四學年4<sup>th</sup> Academic Year</p></td></tr><tr><td><p>上Fall</p></td><td colspan="3"><p>下Spring</p></td><td><p>上Fall</p></td><td><p>下Spring</p></td><td><p>上Fall</p></td><td><p>下Spring</p></td><td><p>上Fall</p></td><td><p>下Spring</p></td></tr><tr><td rowspan="5"><p>共同必修科目Common Compulsory</p><p>（17）</p></td><td><p>中文閱讀、思辨與表達（一）Chinese Reading, Critical Thinking, and Expression （I）</p><p>（2）</p></td><td colspan="3"><p>中文閱讀、思辨與表達（二）Chinese Reading, Critical Thinking, and Expression（II）</p><p>（2）</p></td><td></td><td></td><td></td><td></td><td></td><td></td></tr><tr><td><p>英語（一）</p><p>English （I）</p><p>（2）</p></td><td colspan="3"><p>英語（二）</p><p>English （II）</p><p>（2）</p></td><td></td><td></td><td></td><td></td><td></td><td></td></tr><tr><td colspan="10"><ol><li>外語課程應修習 10 學分。</li><li>「英語（一）」及「英語（二）」為基礎課程，採能力分級上課，共計二學期四學分。</li><li>除了「英語（一）」及「英語（二）」外，畢業前應修畢二個不同主題式英語課程，共計 4 學分。</li><li>大一英語能力後測「TOEIC 模擬測驗」成績未達 350 分者，應修習「應試加強班」（EL260）。修習「應試加強班」期間之期末 TOEIC 模擬測驗成績未達 350 分者，則該科成績將「不及格」，並應再次修習「應試加強班」，直到取得TOEIC模擬測驗分數達 350 分（含）始得修習其他主題式英語課程。</li><li>另開設「英語檢定」（EL160）計一學期2學分，「英語檢定」之修課限制與注意事項，請參照「通識外語『英語檢定』修課規定」，並由通識教學部公佈後施行。</li><li>外國學生可修華語課程10學分，其華語課程 10 學分應含「華語檢定」2 學分，「華語檢定」修課限制與注意事項，請參照「通識外語『英語檢定』修課規定」及「元智大學外籍生華語學分抵免規定」。</li><li>凡本校大學部外國學生修習「華語（一）」或「華語（二）」任一課程成績未達60分，不得修習「華語（三）」、「華語（四）」。若修習「華語（三）」、「華語（四）」任一課程成績未達60分，不得修習「華語檢定」（EL375）。</li></ol><p>1.	The undergraduate students must complete 10 required credits of foreign language courses.</p><p>2.	English (I) &amp; (II) for the total 4 credits: English (I) and (II) are 4 credits elementary courses for the freshmen who are grouped on English competence; to complete within two semesters.</p><p>3.	English thematic course for the total 4 credits: English thematic courses are 4-credit English courses; students are required to obtain 4 credits through 2 different thematic courses for graduation. </p><p>4.	Students who do not reach the 350-point threshold of TOEIC Mock Exam in the end of the freshman year must take English Testing (EL260) course. Students will fail the course if they do not score higher than 350 points of TOEIC Mock Exam by the end of the course, and must repeatedly take the course until they can score higher than 350 points. </p><p>5.	“English Testing” (EL160) is a 2-credit course: For the requirements of registering “English Testing”, please refer to The Regulation for Registering English Test announced and implemented by the College of General Education.</p><p>6.	Foreign students could take 10 credits of Mandarin Chinese courses as alternative courses of English. The 10 credits in Mandarin Chinese courses must include 2 credits for “Chinese Proficiency Test”. For the specific restrictions and considerations for taking the “Chinese Proficiency Test”, please refer to the 'General Education Foreign Language “English Proficiency Exam” Course Requirements' and 'Yuan Ze University Regulations for Exempting the Mandarin Chinese as a Foreign Language Credit ' for more details.</p><p>7. The undergraduate foreign students must pass Mandarin Chinese (I) and (II) before taking Mandarin Chinese (III) and (IV). Students must pass Mandarin Chinese (III) and (IV) before taking 'Chinese Proficiency Test' (EL375).</p><p> 英語檢定English Testing（2）、經典選讀A Guide to Classics（2）、服務學習Service Learning（1）</p></td></tr><tr><td colspan="2"><p>體育Physical Education（0）</p></td><td><p>體育Physical Education（0）</p></td><td colspan="2"><p>興趣選項體育optional physical education（0）</p></td><td><p>興趣選項體育optional physical education（0）</p></td><td></td><td></td><td></td><td></td></tr><tr><td colspan="10"><p>大學部必須修習4學期體育課程；其中2學期為大一體育課程原班級上課，另2學期為興趣選項體育課程。</p><p>The undergraduate students must attend the physical education course for 4 semesters; 2 semesters for the freshman physical education courses, the other two semesters for the optional physical education courses.</p></td></tr><tr><td><p>通識教育科目</p><p>General Education（10）</p></td><td colspan="10"><p>通識課程分為人文藝術、自然科學、社會科學及生命科學四大類。學生須於四大領域中各選修2學分課程，共計8學分。General Education program comprises four categories：Humanities, Natural Science, Social Science and Life Science. Students are required to take a 2-credit course from each category to get 8 credits before graduation.</p><p>通識跨域課程General Education Interdisciplinary Course：此2學分學生可自由於通識講座課程、微課自主學習或在地多元文化課群中選課。惟外籍生與工程學院英語學士班、資訊學院英語學士班、人文社會學院英語學士班、電機通訊學院英語學士班學生仍須於四大領域中選課，依各院修課規定辦理。Students can select the 2 credits from a General Education Lecture course, Micro Credit courses, Self-Study courses, or Local-Multicultural courses. Only foreign students and undergraduates of International Programs in the Colleges of Engineering, Informatics, Humanities and Social Sciences, as well as Electrical and Communication Engineering are required to take a 2-credit course from the four categories according to each college’s policy before graduation.</p></td></tr><tr><td><p>院必修科目</p><p>College</p><p>Compulsory</p><p>（4）</p></td><td><p>HS005</p><p>數位人文應用（一）</p><p>Digital Applications in Humanities I  (2)</p></td><td regulations.</p><ol><li>通識教育科目學分只採計至多10學分，超修之學分將不列入畢業學分。</li></ol><p>The maximum credits for general education courses is 10, the exceeding credits will not be counted.</p><ol><li>【數位編輯實務】(課號CC014) Work] Categorized as the final learning course of faculty, 3 learning hours for the subject with 1 credit point.</li><li>本系課程凡為(一)、(二)/上、下學期開設者，須皆修畢始承認該科學分。<br/>For subjects of faculty that subdivided into parts to be taken on first (1st) and second (2nd) semester, credit points will only be recognized with both semesters completed.</li><li><a></a>核心選修之【文學行旅】及【文化探秘】領域，至少選修8學分，且各領域至少選修1門，以符合本系畢業規定。</li></ol><p>In the core elective fields of " The Literary of Travel " and " The Exploration of Culture ", at least 8 credits must be taken, and at least one course should be taken in each field to meet the requirements.</p><ol><li>核心選修【數位應用】領域之所有課程皆為本系「數位應用相關課程｣，畢業前須通過至少2門(可至本系或外系修習)。</li></ol><p>All courses in the core elective field of "Digital Application " are "Digital Application-related Courses" of our department.Students must pass at least 2 courses before graduation (Students can study in our department or external departments).</p><ol><li>系必修習作課程【詩選及習作】、【詞選及習作】為單班課程，習作課程每學期須制定習作。</li></ol><p>   Compulsory subjects of faculty【Selected Poems with Writing Exercise 】and【Selected Ci with Writing Exercise】are single classes. Assignment needed to be drawn up for each semester.</p><ol><li>本系同學總共必須修滿 130學分方可畢業，包括共同必修及通識課程共27學分、院必修課程共4學分、本系必修43學分，其餘選修56學分（外系選修至多承認17學分，其中包含專業自主學習1-3學分，與他系合作之學程，依學程規定承認最高學分）。</li></ol><p>Student of Dept. of Ad must take 130 credits in total for graduation,include Required Common Courses and General Education courses (27) credits , College Compulsory Courses (4) credits, Department Compulsory courses (43) credits, and Department Elective courses (56) credits.（A maximum of（17）credits can be recognized for free electives, including（1–3）credits for self-directed professional learning. For the cooperation courses with other departments, credits will be recognized according to the specific program regulations.）</p><p>10. 為增進學生英文能力，鼓勵選修英語授課課程(含英專班)，其修習之課程科目及學分數之認抵需依學系規定辦理。</p><p>To improve students’ English, we encourage students to take the courses in English (including English Bachelor), which courses and credits waiver and transference should be standardized by each department.</p><p>11. 自106學年度起軍訓課程由必修改為選修，該學分納入當學期修課學分數計算，但不納入畢業總學分計算。</p><p>The military education courses are no longer compulsory starting the 106 academic year. The military education courses will not be accumulated to the graduation requirements, but they can be counted as taken credits for each semester.</p><p>12. 修習碩士班課程以大三以上學生為限，且不得修習碩士在職專班課程。</p><p>Master's degree courses are limited to students in their third year or above, and students are not allowed to take courses from the Executive Master program.</p></td></tr></table>
```

**元智大學中國語文學系必修科目表**

**Dept. of Chinese Linguistics & Literature, Yuan Ze University**

**List of Required Courses**

**（109學年度入學新生適用Academic Year 2020）**

109.05.06 一○八學年度第六次教務會議通過

Passed by the 6th Academic Affairs Meeting, Academic Year 2019, on May 06, 2020

109.11.11 一○九學年度第二次教務會議修訂通過

Amended by the 2nd Academic Affairs Meeting, Academic Year 2020, on November 11, 2020

(Course Name: Fundamental Computer Programming)</p></td></tr><tr><td colspan="18"><p>外語課程應依「通識外語修課規定」修習，共計10學分。</p><ol><li>「英語（一）」及「英語（二）」為基礎課程，採能力分級上課，共計二學期四學分。</li><li>除了「英語（一）」及「英語（二）」外，應修習主題式英語課程三學期5學分，畢業前需修畢三個不同英語課程，始取得畢業資格。大一英語能力後測TOEIC模擬測驗成績未達350分者，應修習「應試加強班」，修習「應試加強班」期間之期末TOEIC模擬測驗成績未達350分者，則該科成績將「不及格」，並應再次修習「應試加強班」，直到取得TOEIC模擬測驗分數達350分(含)始得修習其他主題式英語課程。</li><li>另開設「英語檢定」計一學期1學分，「英語檢定」之修課限制與注意事項，請參照「英語檢定」修課規定，並由通識教學部公佈後施行。</li></ol><p>外國學生改修華語須經國際語言文化中心審核通過始可改修華語課程10學分，其華語課程10學分應含「華語檢定」1學分，「華語檢定」修課限制與注事意項，請參照「英語檢定」修課規定。</p><p>凡本校大學部外國學生(不含交換生)修習「華語一」或「華語二」任一課程成績未達60分，不得修習「華語三」、「華語四」、「華語五」、「華語六」，若修習「華語三」、「華語四」任一課程成績未達60分，不得修習「華語五」或「華語檢定」。</p><p>The undergraduate students must complete 10 required credits of foreign language courses as follows:</p><ul><li>English (I), (II): 4 credits</li><li>English thematic course: 5 credits </li><li>English Test: 1 credit</li></ul><p>English (I) and (II) are 4 credits elementary courses for the freshmen who are grouped on English competence-based to complete within two semesters.</p><p>English thematic courses are 5-credit of English courses; students are required to obtain </p><p>5 credits through 3 different thematic courses for graduation.</p><p>For the requirements of registering “English Testing”, please refer to "the Regulation for Registering English Test" announced and implemented by the College of General Education.</p><p>Foreign students need approval by ILCC for taking 10 credits of Mandarin Chinese courses as alternative courses of English.</p><p>The undergraduate foreign students, exchange students excluded, must score 60 points or higher to pass Mandarin Chinese (I) and (II) before taking Mandarin Chinese (III), (IV), (V), and (VI). Students must score 60 points or higher in Mandarin Chinese (III) and (IV) before taking Mandarin Chinese (V) and (VI).</p><p>英語檢定English Testing（1）、經典五十Fifty Canonized Books（2）、服務學習Service Learning（1）</p></td></tr><tr><td colspan="2"><p>體育Physical Education（0）</p></td><td colspan="4"><p>體育Physical Education（0）</p></td><td colspan="3"><p>體育Physical Education（0）</p></td><td colspan="3"><p>體育Physical Education（0）</p></td><td colspan="2"></td><td></td><td></td><td colspan="2"></td></tr><tr><td colspan="18"><p>體育除修習大一至大二4個學期外，另需通過「游泳能力檢定」及「心肺適能檢定」等二項檢測，列為畢業門檻。</p><p>Beside taking PE courses for 4 semesters (Year 1 to 2), students must pass both swimming and cardiopulmonary function tests.</p></td></tr><tr><td><p>通識教育科目General Education</p><p>（10）</p></td><td colspan="18"><p>通識課程分為人文藝術、自然科學、社會科學及生命科學四大類。學生須於四大領域中各選修2學分課程，共計8學分。General Education program comprises four categories：Humanities, Natural Science, Social Science and Life Science. Students are required to take a 2-credit course from each category to get 8 credits before graduation.</p><p>通識跨域課程General Education Interdisciplinary Course：此2學分學生可自由於通識講座課程、微課自主學習或在地多元文化課群中選課。惟外籍生與工程學院英語學士班、資訊學院英語學士班、人文社會學院英語學士班、電機通訊學院英語學士班學生仍須於四大領域中選課，依各院修課規定辦理。Students can select the 2 credits from a General Education Lecture course, Micro Credit courses, Self-Study courses, or Local-Multicultural courses. Only foreign students and undergraduates of International Programs in the Colleges of Engineering, Informatics, Humanities and Social Sciences, as well as Electrical and Communication Engineering are required to take a 2-credit course from the four categories according to each college’s policy before graduation.</p></td></tr><tr><td rowspan="4"><p>系必修科目Department Common Required Course List for General Education courses information</p><p>and regulations.</p><ol><li>為增進學生英文能力，鼓勵選修英語授課課程(含英專班)，其修習之課程科目及學分數之認抵需依學系規定辦理。</li></ol><p>To improve students’ English, we encourage students to take the courses in English (including  English Bachelor), which courses and credits waiver and transference should be standardized by each department.</p><ol><li>通識教育科目學分只採計至多10學分，超修之學分將不列入畢業學分。The maximum credits for general education courses is 10, the exceeding credits will not be counted.</li><li>【畢業製作】課程1學分，上課3小時，列為本系終端學習課程。<br/>[Graduation Work] Categorized as the final learning course of faculty, 3 learning hours for the subject with 1 credit point.</li><li>【實務製作】(課號CC395) 3學分為本系必修「議題導向實作」課程。</li></ol><p>Three credits of Practical Work (CC395) is compulsory of topic-oriented implementation course.</p><ol><li>【文獻數位化編輯與應用 】(課號CC174)、【文獻大數據管理與應用】 (課號CC297)、【雲端應用與APP設計】(課號CC391)為本系「數位應用相關課程｣，畢業前須通過至少2門。</li></ol><p>Before graduation, students have to pass at least two courses from below digital courses: Literature Digitization and Editing Applications(CC174), Big Data Management and Application(CC297) and Cloud Application Design and APP(CC391).</p><ol><li>本系必修課程凡分(一)、(二)上下學期開設者，須先修過（一），且學期成績達40分以上，始可修（二）；(一)、(二)上下學期皆修畢者，始承認該科學分。<br/>For compulsory subjects of faculty that subdivided into parts to be taken on first (1st) and second (2nd) semester, students must clear the (1st) semester with 40 credit points and above in order to enter the (2nd) semester; moreover, credit points will only be recognized with both semesters completed.</li><li>系必修習作課程【詩選及習作】、【詞選及習作】為單班課程，習作課程每學期須制定習作。</li></ol><p>   Compulsory subjects of faculty【Selected Poems with Writing Exercise 】and【Selected Ci with Writing Exercise】are single classes. Assignment needed to be drawn up for each semester.</p><ol><li>本系同學總共必須修滿 130學分方可畢業，包括共同必修及通識課程共31學分、本系必修44學分，其餘選修55學分（外系選修至多承認17學分，與他系合作之學程，依學程規定承認最高學分）。</li></ol><p>Student of Dept. of Ad must take 130 credits in total for graduation,include Required Common Courses and General Education courses (31), Department Compulsory courses (44), and Department Elective courses (55). (Outside the Department of elective up to recognize the (17) credits, and the cooperation courses with other departments, according to the provisions of the highest recognition of credit)</p></td></tr></table>
```

clear the (1st) semester in order to enter the (2nd) semester; moreover, credit points will only be recognized with both semesters completed.</li><li>核心選修科目之課程領域須選修8學分。<br/>Students should obtain 8 credit points from core elective subjects in respective field of studies.</li><li>現代詩專題、現代散文專題和現代小說專題三門課，應至少先修一門以下課程：該系列課程的「選讀及習作」或「台灣文學史」、「亞洲華文文學」。<br/>For the 3 courses of Topics on Modern Poetry, Topics on Modern Prose and Topics on Modern Novel, students have to complete at least one of its subdivided subject: the “selected readings and writing” of respective courses; or “History of Taiwanese Literature”, or “Asian Chinese Literature”.</li><li>【文獻數位化編輯與應用 】(課號CC174)、【文獻大數據管理與應用】 (課號CC297)、【雲端應用與APP設計】(課號CC391)為本系「數位應用相關課程｣，畢業前須通過至少2門(可至本系或外系修習)。</li></ol><p>Before graduation, students have to pass at least two courses from below digital courses: Literature Digitization and Editing Applications(CC174), Big Data Management and Application(CC297) and Cloud Application Design and APP(CC391). (Student may take 'digital application courses' from another department.) .</p></td></tr></table>

AA-CP-04-CF05 (1.2 版)／101.11.15 修訂

completed.</li><li><a></a>核心選修之【文學行旅】及【文化探秘】領域，至少選修8學分，且各領域至少選修1門，以符合本系畢業規定。</li></ol><p>In the core elective fields of " The Literary of Travel " and " The Exploration of Culture ", at least 8 credits must be taken, and at least one course should be taken in each field to meet the requirements.</p><ol><li>核心選修【數位應用】領域之所有課程皆為本系「數位應用相關課程｣，畢業前須通過至少2門(可至本系或外系修習)。</li></ol><p>All courses in the core elective field of "Digital Application " are "Digital Application-related Courses" of our department.Students must pass at least 2 courses before graduation (Students can study in our department or external departments).</p></td></tr></table>
```

<!-- OCR_END -->

Topics on Modern Prose and Topics on Modern Novel, students have to complete at least one of its subdivided subject: the “selected readings and writing” of respective courses; or “History of Taiwanese Literature”, or “Asian Chinese Literature”.</li><li>【文獻數位化編輯與應用 】(課號CC174)、【文獻大數據管理與應用】 (課號CC297)、【雲端應用與APP設計】(課號CC391)為本系「數位應用相關課程｣，畢業前須通過至少2門(可至本系或外系修習)。</li></ol><p>Before graduation, students have to pass at least two courses from below digital courses: Literature Digitization and Editing Applications(CC174), Big Data Management and Application(CC297) and Cloud Application Design and APP(CC391). (Student may take 'digital application courses' from another department.) .</p></td></tr></table>

AA-CP-04-CF05 (1.2 版)／101.11.15 修訂

**元智大學 中國語文學系 擋修科目表**

**Dep. of Chinese Linguistics & Literature, Yuan Ze University**

**List of Prerequisites Courses**

**（105學年度入學新生適用Applied to Students of Academic Year 105）**

105.04.20一○四學年度第五次教務會議通過

<table><tr><td colspan="2"><p>先修科目 Prerequisites</p></td><td><p>擋修科目 Prerequisites</p></td><td rowspan="2"><p>備註 Remarks</p></td></tr><tr><td><p>課名 Course Name</p></td><td><p>分數 Score</p></td><td><p>課名 Course Name</p></td></tr><tr><td><p>語言學概論（一）</p><p>Introduction of Linguistics(I)</p></td><td><p>40</p></td><td><p>語言學概論（二）</p><p>Introduction of Linguistics(II)</p></td><td></td></tr><tr><td><p>現代文學創意習作（一）</p><p>A Selection of Modern Chinese Literature and Creative Writing(I)</p></td><td><p>40</p></td><td><p>現代文學創意習作（二）</p><p>A Selection of Modern Chinese Literature and Creative Writing(II)</p></td><td></td></tr><tr><td><p>二十世紀中國文學史（一）</p><p>History of Chinese Twentieth Century Literature(I)</p></td><td><p>40</p></td><td><p>二十世紀中國文學史（二）</p><p>History of Chinese Twentieth Century Literature(II)</p></td><td></td></tr><tr><td><p>中國文學史（一）</p><p>History of Chinese Literature(I)</p></td><td><p>40</p></td><td><p>中國文學史（二）</p><p>History of Chinese Literature(II)</p></td><td></td></tr><tr><td><p>詩選及習作(一)</p><p>Selected Poems with Writing Exercise(I)</p></td><td><p>40</p></td><td><p>詩選及習作(二)</p><p>Selected Poems with Writing Exercise(II)</p></td><td></td></tr><tr><td><p>詞選及習作(一)</p><p>Selected Ci with Writing Exercise(I)</p></td><td><p>40</p></td><td><p>詞選及習作(二)</p><p>Selected Ci with Writing Exercise(I)</p></td><td></td></tr><tr><td><p>中國思想史（一）</p><p>History of Chinese Philosophy(I)</p></td><td><p>40</p></td><td><p>中國思想史（二）</p><p>History of Chinese Philosophy(II)</p></td><td></td></tr></table>

- 本系凡分(一)、 (二)上下學期開設之必修課程，均須先修習（一），始得修習（二），上下學期皆修畢者，始承認該科學分。
For compulsory subjects of faculty that subdivided into parts to be taken on first (1<sup>st</sup>) and second (2<sup>nd</sup>) semester; credit points will only be recognized with both semesters completed.
- 本系必修課程，上學期總成績未達40分者，不得續修下學期。
For compulsory subjects of faculty, students must score 40 marks and above before joining the next semester.
- 自113學年度起凡本系開設之必選修課程，取消「 (一)、(二)上下學期課程，須先修過（一），且學期成績達40分以上，始可修（二）」之規定，本系所有課程皆不設擋修。

Starting from the 113th academic year, all compulsory elective courses offered by the department will be abolished, and the requirement of "(1) and (2) courses in the first and second semesters must be taken first and the semester score of 40 points or above can be taken (2)", and all courses of the department will not be blocked.

AA-CP-04-CF08 (1.2 版)／101.11.15 修訂

```markdown
**元智大學中國語文學系 輔系科目表**

**Dep. of Chinese Linguistics & Literature,** Yuan Ze University List of Minor Courses

**（** 105學年度申請適用**Applied to Students of Academic Year 105）**

105.04.20 一○四學年第五次教務會議通過

Passed by the 5th Academic Affairs Meeting, Academic Year 2016, on April 22, 2016

<table><tr><td><p><strong>輔系名稱</strong>Minor in</p></td><td><p><strong>輔系科目</strong>Minor Courses</p></td><td><p>學分 Credit</p></td><td><p>備註 Remarks</p></td></tr><tr><td rowspan="5"><p>中國語文學系</p><p><strong>Dep. of Chinese Linguistics &amp; Literatur</strong></p></td><td><p>中國文學史(一) History of Chinese Literature(I)</p></td><td><p>3</p></td><td rowspan="4"><p>必修課程</p><p>Compulsory</p></td></tr><tr><td><p>中國文學史(二) History of Chinese Literature(II)</p></td><td><p>3</p></td></tr><tr><td><p>中國思想史(一) History of Chinese Philosophy(I)</p></td><td><p>3</p></td></tr><tr><td><p>中國思想史(二) History of Chinese Philosophy(II)</p></td><td><p>3</p></td></tr><tr><td><p>以中語系105學年度之必、選修科目表為準，開放學生自由選課。<br/>Based on compulsory and elective subjects from Faculty of Chinese Studies in year 2016; free choices opened for all students.</p></td><td><p>15</p></td><td><p>選修課程</p><p>Elective</p></td></tr></table>

註：1、選修本系為輔系之學生必須修滿27學分（含）以上，才予以承認其輔系資格。

An individual student who minors in Information Management must undertake courses offered within the Department up to 27 credits and above before he/she can have the minor admitted.

2、學生應修習【中國文學史】、【中國思想史】兩門必修課程，共計12學分。
Students should attend the two compulsory subjects - “History of Chinese Literature” and “History of Chinese Philosophy” with 12 credit points.

3、其餘15學分，學生可於該年度之必、選修科目表中擇課修習。
Students could obtain the remaining 15 credit points from other compulsory and elective subjects on particular year.

AA-CP-04-CF09 (1.3 版)／104.01.06 修訂
```

**Dept. of Chinese Linguistics & Literature, Yuan Ze University**

**List of Minor Courses**

107.05.02 一○六學年度第五次教務會議通過

Passed by the 5th Academic Affairs Meeting, Academic Year 2017, on May 2, 2018

<table><tr><td><p><strong><em>輔系名稱</em></strong><em>Minor in</em></p></td><td><p><strong>輔系科目</strong>Minor Courses</p></td><td><p>學分 Credit</p></td><td><p>備註 Remarks</p></td></tr><tr><td rowspan="5"><p><em>中國語文學系</em></p><p><strong><em>Dep. of Chinese Linguistics &amp; Literatur</em></strong></p></td><td><p>中國文學史(一) History of Chinese Literature(I)</p></td><td><p>3</p></td><td rowspan="4"><p>必修課程</p><p>Compulsory</p></td></tr><tr><td><p>中國文學史(二) History of Chinese Literature(II)</p></td><td><p>3</p></td></tr><tr><td><p>中國思想史(一) History of Chinese Philosophy(I)</p></td><td><p>3</p></td></tr><tr><td><p>中國思想史(二) History of Chinese Philosophy(II)</p></td><td><p>3</p></td></tr><tr><td><p>以中語系107學年度之必、選修科目表為準，開放學生自由選課。<br/>Based on compulsory and elective subjects from Faculty of Chinese Linguistics and Literature in year 2018; free choices opened for all students.</p></td><td><p>15</p></td><td><p>選修課程</p><p>Elective</p></td></tr></table>

註：1、選修本系為輔系之學生必須修滿27學分（含）以上，才予以承認其輔系資格。

An individual student who minors in Information Management must undertake courses offered within the Department up to 27 credits and above before he/she can have the minor admitted.

2、學生應修習【中國文學史】、【中國思想史】兩門必修課程，共計12學分。
Students should attend the two compulsory subjects - “History of Chinese Literature” and “History of Chinese Philosophy” with 12 credit points.

3、其餘15學分，學生可於該年度之必、選修科目表中擇課修習。
Students could obtain the remaining 15 credit points from other compulsory and elective subjects on particular year.

AA-CP-04-CF09 (1.3 版)／104.01.06 修訂
```

**元智大學中國語文學系 輔系科目表**

**Dept. of Chinese Linguistics & Literature, Yuan Ze University**

**List of Minor Courses**

106.04.26 一○五學年度第五次教務會議通過

Passed by the 5th Academic Affairs Meeting, Academic Year 2016, on April 26, 2017

<table><tr><td><p><strong>輔系名稱</strong>Minor in</p></td><td><p><strong>輔系科目</strong>Minor Courses</p></td><td><p>學分 Credit</p></td><td><p>備註 Remarks</p></td></tr><tr><td rowspan="5"><p>中國語文學系</p><p><strong>Dep. of Chinese Linguistics &amp; Literatur</strong></p></td><td><p>中國文學史(一) History of Chinese Literature(I)</p></td><td><p>3</p></td><td rowspan="4"><p>必修課程</p><p>Compulsory</p></td></tr><tr><td><p>中國文學史(二) History of Chinese Literature(II)</p></td><td><p>3</p></td></tr><tr><td><p>中國思想史(一) History of Chinese Philosophy(I)</p></td><td><p>3</p></td></tr><tr><td><p>中國思想史(二) History of Chinese Philosophy(II)</p></td><td><p>3</p></td></tr><tr><td><p>以中語系106學年度之必、選修科目表為準，開放學生自由選課。<br/>Based on compulsory and elective subjects from Faculty of Chinese Linguistics and Literature in year 2017; free choices opened for all students.</p></td><td><p>15</p></td><td><p>選修課程</p><p>Elective</p></td></tr></table>

註：1、選修本系為輔系之學生必須修滿27學分（含）以上，才予以承認其輔系資格。

An individual student who minors in Information Management must undertake courses offered within the Department up to 27 credits and above before he/she can have the minor admitted.

2、學生應修習【中國文學史】、【中國思想史】兩門必修課程，共計12學分。
Students should attend the two compulsory subjects - “History of Chinese Literature” and “History of Chinese Philosophy” with 12 credit points.

3、其餘15學分，學生可於該年度之必、選修科目表中擇課修習。
Students could obtain the remaining 15 credit points from other compulsory and elective subjects on particular year.

AA-CP-04-CF09 (1.3 版)／104.01.06 修訂
```

**元智大學中國語文學系碩士班  必修科目表**

**Master Program of Chinese Linguistics & Literature, Yuan Ze University**

**List of Required Courses**

**（105學年度入學新生適用Applied to Students of Academic Year 105）**

105.04.20一○四學年度第五次教務會議通過

Approved by the 5th Academic Affairs Meeting, Academic Year 105, on April 20, 2016

105.11.09 一○五學年度第二次教務會議修訂通過

Amended by the 2nd Academic Affairs Meeting, Academic Year 2016, on November 09, 2016

<table><tr><td rowspan="2"><p>     學年Academic Year</p><p>學期Semester</p><p>科目Subject </p></td><td colspan="2"><p>第一學年 1<sup>st</sup> Academic Year</p></td><td colspan="2"><p>第二學年 2<sup>nd</sup> Academic Year</p></td></tr><tr><td><p>上Fall</p></td><td><p>下Spring</p></td><td><p>上Fall</p></td><td><p>下Spring</p></td></tr><tr><td><p>必</p><p>修</p><p>科</p><p>目</p><p>Compulsory</p><p>（4）</p></td><td><p> CC546</p><p>論文寫作（一）</p><p>Thesis Writing(I)</p><p>（2）</p></td><td><p>CC547</p><p>論文寫作（二）</p><p>Thesis Writing(II)</p><p>（2）</p></td><td><p> </p></td><td></td></tr><tr><td><p>學期</p><p>學分小計</p><p>Credits each semester</p></td><td><p>2</p></td><td><p>2</p></td><td></td><td></td></tr><tr><td><p>備</p><p>註</p></td><td colspan="4"><p>1：修業年限：1~4年。<br/>Duration of studies: 1-4 years</p><p>2：最低畢業學分數為24學分，不包括碩士論文。<br/>The minimum graduation score is 24 credits, not including the master's thesis.</p><p>3：依據元智大學學則規定，學生學業成績採百分記分法核計，以一百分為滿分，碩、博士班研究生以七十分為及格。<br/>According to the provisions of the Yuan Ze University, Percentile Score Method was used to evaluate the academic achievement of students, whereas 100 marks is the full score, and 70 is the passing score for master and doctoral graduate students.</p><p>4：【論文寫作（一）】未達60分者，不得續修【論文寫作（二）】。<br/>Student must score 60 marks and above in “Thesis Writing (1)”, in order to proceed to “Thesis Writing (2)”.</p><p>5：依據本校「學術研究倫理教育課程實施要點」，入學研究生須依本校學術研究倫理教育課程實施要點規定，於入學第一學期結束前完成學術研究倫理教育課程，最遲須於申請學位口試前補修完成，未完成本課程，不得申請學位口試。<br/>With reference to “Key Points in Implementation of Ethical Education Curriculum in Academic Research”, postgraduate students must obey the provisions of Key Points in Implementation of Ethical Education Curriculum in Academic Research, to complete the Ethical Education Curriculum in Academic Research, latest before the oral test of degree’s application; or otherwise the application of oral test for degree course would not be accepted.</p><p>6: 另須依據元智大學中國語文學系碩士班修業規定完成學位考試。<br/>In addition, degree examination shall be completed in accordance with the requirements of the Master Program of Faculty of Chinese Language of Yuan Ze University.</p></td></tr></table>

AA-CP-04-CF03 (1.2 版)／101.11.15 修訂

**元智大學中國語文學系碩士班  必修科目表**

**Master Program of Chinese Linguistics & Literature, Yuan Ze University**

**List of Required Courses**

**（107學年度入學新生適用Applied to Students of Academic Year 2018）**

107.05.02 一○六學年度第五次教務會議通過

Passed by the 5th Academic Affairs Meeting, Academic Year 2017, on May 2, 2018

<table><tr><td rowspan="2"><p>     學年Academic Year</p><p>學期Semester</p><p>科目Subject </p></td><td colspan="2"><p>第一學年 1<sup>st</sup> Academic Year</p></td><td colspan="2"><p>第二學年 2<sup>nd</sup> Academic Year</p></td></tr><tr><td><p>上Fall</p></td><td><p>下Spring</p></td><td><p>上Fall</p></td><td><p>下Spring</p></td></tr><tr><td><p>必</p><p>修</p><p>科</p><p>目</p><p>Compulsory</p><p>（4）</p></td><td><p> CC546</p><p>論文寫作（一）</p><p>Thesis Writing(I)</p><p>（2）</p></td><td><p>CC547</p><p>論文寫作（二）</p><p>Thesis Writing(II)</p><p>（2）</p></td><td><p> </p></td><td></td></tr><tr><td><p>學期</p><p>學分小計</p><p>Credits each semester</p></td><td><p>2</p></td><td><p>2</p></td><td></td><td></td></tr><tr><td><p>備</p><p>註</p><p>Remarks</p></td><td colspan="4"><p>1：修業年限：1~4年。<br/>Duration of studies: 1-4 years</p><p>2：最低畢業學分數為24學分，不包括碩士論文。<br/>The minimum graduation score is 24 credits, not including the master's thesis.</p><p>3：依據元智大學學則規定，學生學業成績採百分記分法核計，以一百分為滿分，碩、博士班研究生以七十分為及格。<br/>According to the provisions of the Yuan Ze University, Percentile Score Method was used to evaluate the academic achievement of students, whereas 100 marks is the full score, and 70 is the passing score for master and doctoral graduate students.</p><p>4：未修習【論文寫作（一）】，不得續修【論文寫作（二）】。<br/>Student must take “Thesis Writing (1)”, in order to proceed to “Thesis Writing (2)”.</p><p>5：依據本校「學術研究倫理教育課程實施要點」，入學研究生須依本校學術研究倫理教育課程實施要點規定，於入學第一學期結束前完成學術研究倫理教育課程，最遲須於申請學位口試前補修完成，未完成本課程，不得申請學位口試。<br/>With reference to “Key Points in Implementation of Ethical Education Curriculum in Academic Research”, postgraduate students must obey the provisions of Key Points in Implementation of Ethical Education Curriculum in Academic Research, to complete the Ethical Education Curriculum in Academic Research, latest before the oral test of degree’s application; or otherwise the application of oral test for degree course would not be accepted.</p><p>6: 另須依據元智大學中國語文學系碩士班修業規定完成學位考試。<br/>In addition, degree examination shall be completed in accordance with the requirements of the Master Program of Faculty of Chinese Language of Yuan Ze University.</p></td></tr></table>

AA-CP-04-CF03 (1.2 版)／101.11.15 修訂
```

**Master Program of Chinese Linguistics & Literature, Yuan Ze University**

**List of Required Courses**

**（109學年度入學新生適用Academic Year 2020）**

109.05.06 一○八學年度第六次教務會議通過

Passed by the 6th Academic Affairs Meeting, Academic Year 2019, on May 06, 2020

<table><tr><td rowspan="2"><p>     學年Academic Year</p><p>學期Semester</p><p>科目Subject </p></td><td colspan="2"><p>第一學年 1<sup>st</sup> Academic Year</p></td><td colspan="2"><p>第二學年 2<sup>nd</sup> Academic Year</p></td></tr><tr><td><p>上Fall</p></td><td><p>下Spring</p></td><td><p>上Fall</p></td><td><p>下Spring</p></td></tr><tr><td><p>必</p><p>修</p><p>科</p><p>目</p><p>Compulsory</p><p>（2）</p></td><td><p> CC561</p><p>論文寫作</p><p>Thesis Writing</p><p>（2）</p></td><td></td><td><p> </p></td><td></td></tr><tr><td><p>學期</p><p>學分小計</p><p>Credits each semester</p></td><td><p>2</p></td><td></td><td></td><td></td></tr><tr><td><p>備</p><p>註</p><p>Remarks</p></td><td colspan="4"><p>1：修業年限：1~4年。Duration of studies: 1-4 years</p><p>2：最低畢業學分數為24學分，不包括碩士論文。<br/>The minimum graduation score is 24 credits, not including the master's thesis.</p><p>3：依據元智大學學則規定，學生學業成績採百分記分法核計，以一百分為滿分，碩、博士班研究生以七十分為及格。<br/>According to the provisions of the Yuan Ze University, Percentile Score Method was used to evaluate the academic achievement of students, whereas 100 marks is the full score, and 70 is the passing score for master and doctoral graduate students.</p><p>4：依據本校「學術研究倫理教育課程實施要點」，入學研究生須依本校學術研究倫理教育課程實施要點規定，於入學第一學期結束前完成學術研究倫理教育課程，最遲須於申請學位口試前補修完成，未完成本課程，不得申請學位口試。<br/>With reference to “Key Points in Implementation of Ethical Education Curriculum in Academic Research”, postgraduate students must obey the provisions of Key Points in Implementation of Ethical Education Curriculum in Academic Research, to complete the Ethical Education Curriculum in Academic Research, latest before the oral test of degree’s application; or otherwise the application of oral test for degree course would not be accepted.</p><p>5: 另須依據元智大學中國語文學系碩士班修業規定完成學位考試。<br/>In addition, degree examination shall be completed in accordance with the requirements of the Master Program of Faculty of Chinese Language of Yuan Ze University.</p></td></tr></table>

Passed by the 5th Academic Affairs Meeting, Academic Year 2020, on May 05, 2021

<table><tr><td rowspan="2"><p>     學年Academic Year</p><p>學期Semester</p><p>科目Subject </p></td><td colspan="2"><p>第一學年 1<sup>st</sup> Academic Year</p></td><td colspan="2"><p>第二學年 2<sup>nd</sup> Academic Year</p></td></tr><tr><td><p>上Fall</p></td><td><p>下Spring</p></td><td><p>上Fall</p></td><td><p>下Spring</p></td></tr><tr><td><p>必</p><p>修</p><p>科</p><p>目</p><p>Compulsory</p><p>(2)</p></td><td><p> CC561</p><p>論文寫作</p><p>Thesis Writing</p><p>(2)</p></td><td></td><td><p> </p></td><td></td></tr><tr><td><p>學期</p><p>學分小計</p><p>Credits each semester</p></td><td><p>2</p></td><td></td><td></td><td></td></tr><tr><td><p>備</p><p>註</p><p>Remarks</p></td><td colspan="4"><p>1：修業年限：1~4年。Duration of studies: 1-4 years</p><p>2：最低畢業學分數為24學分，不包括碩士論文。<br/>The minimum graduation score is 24 credits, not including the master's thesis.</p><p>3：依據元智大學學則規定，學生學業成績採百分記分法核計，以一百分為滿分，碩、博士班研究生以七十分為及格。<br/>According to the provisions of the Yuan Ze University, Percentile Score Method was used to evaluate the academic achievement of students, whereas 100 marks is the full score, and 70 is the passing score for master and doctoral graduate students.</p><p>4：依據本校「學術研究倫理教育課程實施要點」，入學研究生須依本校學術研究倫理教育課程實施要點規定，於入學第一學期結束前完成學術研究倫理教育課程，最遲須於申請學位口試前補修完成，未完成本課程，不得申請學位口試。<br/>With reference to “Key Points in Implementation of Ethical Education Curriculum in Academic Research”, postgraduate students must obey the provisions of Key Points in Implementation of Ethical Education Curriculum in Academic Research, to complete the Ethical Education Curriculum in Academic Research, latest before the oral test of degree’s application; or otherwise the application of oral test for degree course would not be accepted.</p><p>5: 另須依據元智大學中國語文學系碩士班修業規定完成學位考試。<br/>In addition, degree examination shall be completed in accordance with the requirements of the Master Program of Faculty of Chinese Language of Yuan Ze University.</p></td></tr></table>

AA-CP-04-CF03 (1.2 版)／101.11.15 修訂

Passed by the 5th Academic Affairs Meeting, Academic Year 2024, on April 23, 2025

<table><tr><td rowspan="2"><p>學年</p><p>Academic Year</p><p>學期</p><p>Semester</p><p>科目</p><p>Course</p></td><td colspan="2"><p>第一學年</p><p>1<sup>st</sup> Academic Year</p></td><td colspan="2"><p>第二學年</p><p>2<sup>nd</sup> Academic Year</p></td></tr><tr><td><p>上Fall</p></td><td><p>下Spring</p></td><td><p>上Fall</p></td><td><p>下Spring</p></td></tr><tr><td><p>必修科目</p><p>Required Course</p></td><td><p>CC569</p><p>研究方法</p><p>Research Methodology (3)</p></td><td></td><td></td><td></td></tr><tr><td><p>學期學分小計Credits Each Semester</p></td><td><p>3</p></td><td></td><td></td><td></td></tr><tr><td><p>備註</p><p>Remarks</p></td><td colspan="4"><p> 1：修業年限：1~4年。</p><p>Duration of studies: 1-4 years</p><p> 2：最低畢業學分數為24學分，本系必修3學分，其餘選修21學分，不包括碩士論文。</p><p>The minimum graduation score is 24 credits, Department Compulsory courses (3) credits, and Department Elective courses (21) credits, not including the master's thesis.</p><p> 3：選修科目最多9學分可於外系或外校修課，須經導師或指導教授同意；本系有開設之課程一律不允許至外系或外校修課。</p><p>Students can get 9 elective credits at most from other departments or universities with approval by their tutor or advisor.Courses offered by our department cannot be taken in external departments or schools.</p><p> 4：依據元智大學學則規定，學生學業成績採百分記分法核計，以一百分為滿分，碩、博士班研究生以七十分為及格。<br/>According to the provisions of the Yuan Ze University, Percentile Score Method was used to evaluate the academic achievement of students, whereas 100 marks is the full score, and 70 is the passing score for master and doctoral graduate students.</p><p> 5：依據本校「學術研究倫理教育課程實施要點」，入學研究生須依本校學術研究倫理教育課程實施要點規定，於入學第一學期結束前完成學術研究倫理教育課程，最遲須於申請學位口試前補修完成，未完成本課程，不得申請學位口試。<br/>With reference to “Key Points in Implementation of Ethical Education Curriculum in Academic Research”, postgraduate students must obey the provisions of Key Points in Implementation of Ethical Education Curriculum in Academic Research, to complete the Ethical Education Curriculum in Academic Research, latest before the oral test of degree’s application; or otherwise the application of oral test for degree course would not be accepted.</p><p>6:另須依據元智大學中國語文學系碩士班修業規定完成學位考試。<br/>In addition, degree examination shall be completed in accordance with the requirements of the Master Program of Faculty of Chinese Language of Yuan Ze University.</p></td></tr></table>
```

```markdown
元智大學中國語文學系碩士班修業規定

112.04.19 一一一學年度第六次教務會議通過

Passed by the 6th Academic Affairs Meeting, Academic Year 2022, on April 19, 2023

112.10.25 一一二學年度第四次教務會議修訂通過

Amended by the 4th Academic Affairs Meeting, Academic Year 2023, on October 25, 2023

第一條  元智大學中國語文學系(以下簡稱本系)碩士班研究生修業年限一至四年，學生依其入學年度必、選修科目表之相關規定，修滿應修學分，並通過學位考試後授予碩士學位。

第二條  本系研究生最遲須於入學後第一學年結束前確認論文指導教授，並繳交論文指導教授申請表。碩士論文指導教授須為本系專任教師（助理教授級以上）；因論文研究需要，必須先經系內指導教授同意，才得增加一名外系或校外教師（助理教授級以上）共同指導。

第三條  本系研究生得於修業第二學年結束前申請變更論文指導教授，惟須分別經原任與新任指導教授同意，填妥更換論文指導教授申請表，送請系所核備。

第四條  本系學位考試分為學位論文與創作文集兩類。以創作文集申請學位考試之學生，須於大學或碩士就學期間獲全國或縣市政府文學創作獎項及大學校園文學獎各一次。

第五條  選擇學位論文作為學位考試依據者，考試申請前須通過下述規定，並保留各項證明於學位考試申請時繳交。

（一）參加校外學術研討會

研究生在學期間，除參與本系演講、研討會外，必須參加校外研討會至少六次。若遇重大情事（如疫情、天災等不可抗力因素）得彈性調整，相關規定將隨時公告。

（二）碩士論文研究計畫發表

研究生須於第一學年下學期結束前完成碩士論文研究計畫發表。學生研究計畫須符合系所專業領域，通過本系教師檢核後，繳交論文開題審核表。

（三）論文發表

研究生在學期間應於國內外學術期刊或學術會議上發表論文（至少一篇）。核定標準如下：

1.學術期刊：各類研究生學報期刊或學術性期刊

2.學術會議：由大學、學會（含研究生學會）、研究機構舉辦之會議。

第六條  選擇創作文集作為學位考試依據者，學位考試申請前須通過下述規定，並保留各項證明於學位考試申請時繳交。

（一）參加校外學術研討會

研究生在學期間，除參與本系演講、研討會外，必須參加校外研討會至少六次。若遇重大情事（如疫情、天災等不可抗力因素）得彈性調整，相關規定將隨時公告。

（二）通過創作文集計畫及篇章試寫

第一學年結束前須提出創作文集計畫及試寫篇章（散文、小說類約一萬字，新詩十首），經校外委員審查通過，續送系務會議審核是否符合系所專業領域，核定後繳交創作計畫審核表。

（三）論文發表

研究生在學期間應於國內外學術期刊或學術會議上發表論文（至少一篇）。核定標準如下：

1.學術期刊：各類研究生學報期刊或學術性期刊

2.學術會議：由大學、學會（含研究生學會）、研究機構舉辦之會議。

第七條  通過學位考試申請檢核者，得依當學期規定時間至portal申請學位考試，同時繳交學位考試申請表、論文指導教授推薦函及上述相關證明。上學期口試結束日期為 12 月 31 日；下學期口試結束日期為 6 月 30 日。

第八條  研究生應於學位考試前完成論文原創性比對，填寫學位論文原創性比對檢核表，併附Turnitin原創性比對報告書送交指導教授簽章，並於學位考試當日將論文原創性比對報告書送交指導教授及學位考試委員參考。學位論文定稿後亦須完成論文原創性比對，併附Turnitin原創性比對報告書由指導教授審閱核可後，繳交學位論文上傳審核申請表，始可上傳論文。

學位論文比對相似度指標，排除目錄、緒論、參考文獻、附錄等，檢核比對結果之原創性總相似度應低於25%，超過者需敘明原因並由指導教授確認是否屬實。

第九條  通過學位考試之研究生於當學期最後一日（上學期 1 月 31 日；下學期 7 月 31 日）前須完成電子學位論文全文建檔作業，並繳交論文二本，逾期視同下學期畢業。已通過口試之論文或創作文集，如該生遲至修業年限屆滿仍未上傳者，將予以退學。

第十條  學位考試「重考」以一次為限，重考成績仍不及格者，依本校學位考試細則應令退學。

第十一條  提出學位考試申請之研究生，因故無法於學期末前完成考試，研究生應於學期末前提出撤銷申請，逾期或未提出撤銷者，以該次考試失敗論，二次考試失敗依規定予以退學。

第十二條  本系研究生須履行本系訂定之義務與責任，兼領獎、助學金之研究生，需負擔本系安排之助教或行政助理性質之工作。其工作內容包括擔任招生宣傳、系務活動支援、系圖書室值班、協助監考、成績統計及大學部課業輔導等工作。

第十三條  本規定經系課程委員會議通過後，提院課程委員會議、校課程委員會議及教務會議通過後實施，修正時亦同。

元智大學中國語文學系碩士班修業規定

(112學年度入學新生適用) （現行條文）

112.03.14 中語系111-3 次系課程委員會通過

112.03.21中語系111-4 次系課程委員會修訂通過

第一條  元智大學中國語文學系(以下簡稱本系)碩士班研究生修業年限一至四年，學生依其入學年度必、選修科目表之相關規定，修滿應修學分，並通過學位考試後授予碩士學位。

第二條  本系研究生最遲須於入學後第一學年結束前確認論文指導教授，並繳交論文指導教授申請表。碩士論文指導教授須為本系專任教師（助理教授級以上）；因論文研究需要，必須先經系內指導教授同意，才得增加一名外系或校外教師（助理教授級以上）共同指導。

第三條  五年一貫預備研究生通過入學考試後須辦理學分抵免，並於第一學年上學期（ 1 月 31 日）前確認指導教授並繳交論文指導教授申請表。

第四條  本系研究生得於修業第二學年結束前申請變更論文指導教授，惟須分別經原任與新任指導教授同意，填妥更換論文指導教授申請表，送請系所核備。

第五條  本系學位考試分為學位論文與創作文集兩類。以創作文集申請學位考試之學生，須於大學或碩士就學期間獲全國或縣市政府文學創作獎項及大學校園文學獎各一次。

第六條  選擇學位論文作為學位考試依據者，考試申請前須通過下述規定，並保留各項證明於學位考試申請時繳交。

（一）參加校外學術研討會

研究生在學期間，除參與本系演講、研討會外，必須參加校外研討會至少六次。若遇重大情事（如疫情、天災等不可抗力因素）得彈性調整，相關規定將隨時公告。

（二）碩士論文研究計畫發表

研究生須於第一學年下學期結束前完成碩士論文研究計畫發表。學生研究計畫須符合系所專業領域，通過本系教師檢核後，繳交論文開題審核表。

（三）論文發表

研究生在學期間應於國內外學術期刊或學術會議上發表論文（至少一篇）。核定標準如下：

1.學術期刊：各類研究生學報期刊或學術性期刊

2.學術會議：由大學、學會（含研究生學會）、研究機構舉辦之會議。

第七條  選擇創作文集作為學位考試依據者，學位考試申請前須通過下述規定，並保留各項證明於學位考試申請時繳交。

（一）參加校外學術研討會

研究生在學期間，除參與本系演講、研討會外，必須參加校外研討會至少六次。若遇重大情事（如疫情、天災等不可抗力因素）得彈性調整，相關規定將隨時公告。

（二）通過創作文集計畫及篇章試寫

第一學年結束前須提出創作文集計畫及試寫篇章（散文、小說類約一萬字，新詩十首），經校外委員審查通過，續送系務會議審核是否符合系所專業領域，核定後繳交創作計畫審核表。

（三）論文發表

研究生在學期間應於國內外學術期刊或學術會議上發表論文（至少一篇）。核定標準如下：

1.學術期刊：各類研究生學報期刊或學術性期刊

2.學術會議：由大學、學會（含研究生學會）、研究機構舉辦之會議。

第八條  通過學位考試申請檢核者，得依當學期規定時間至portal申請學位考試，同時繳交學位考試申請表、論文指導教授推薦函及上述相關證明。上學期口試結束日期為 12 月 31 日；下學期口試結束日期為 6 月 30 日。

第九條  研究生應於學位考試前完成論文原創性比對，填寫學位論文原創性比對檢核表，併附Turnitin原創性比對報告書送交指導教授簽章，並於學位考試當日將論文原創性比對報告書送交指導教授及學位考試委員參考。學位論文定稿後亦須完成論文原創性比對，併附Turnitin原創性比對報告書由指導教授審閱核可後，繳交學位論文上傳審核申請表，始可上傳論文。

學位論文比對相似度指標，排除目錄、緒論、參考文獻、附錄等，檢核比對結果之原創性總相似度應低於25%，超過者需敘明原因並由指導教授確認是否屬實。

第十條  通過學位考試之研究生於當學期最後一日（上學期 1 月 31 日；下學期 7 月 31 日）前須完成電子學位論文全文建檔作業，並繳交論文二本，逾期視同下學期畢業。已通過口試之論文或創作文集，如該生遲至修業年限屆滿仍未上傳者，將予以退學。

第十一條  學位考試「重考」以一次為限，重考成績仍不及格者，依本校學位考試細則應令退學。

第十二條  提出學位考試申請之研究生，因故無法於學期末前完成考試，研究生應於學期末前提出撤銷申請，逾期或未提出撤銷者，以該次考試失敗論，二次考試失敗依規定予以退學。

第十三條  本系研究生須履行本系訂定之義務與責任，兼領獎、助學金之研究生，需負擔本系安排之助教或行政助理性質之工作。其工作內容包括擔任招生宣傳、系務活動支援、系圖書室值班、協助監考、成績統計及大學部課業輔導等工作。

第十四條  本規定經系課程委員會議通過後，提院課程委員會議、校課程委員會議及教務會議通過後實施，修正時亦同。

**元智大學 中國語文學系碩士班 擋修科目表**

**（105學年度入學新生適用）**

105.04.20一○四學年度第五次教務會議通過

<table><tr><td colspan="2"><p>先修科目</p></td><td><p>擋修科目</p></td><td rowspan="2"><p>備註</p></td></tr><tr><td><p>課名</p></td><td><p>分數</p></td><td><p>課名</p></td></tr><tr><td><p>論文寫作（一） </p></td><td><p>60</p></td><td><p>論文寫作（二）</p></td><td></td></tr></table>

- 本系凡分(一)、 (二)上下學期開設之必修課程，均須先修習（一），始得修習（二），上下學期皆修畢者，始承認該科學分。
- 本系必修課程，上學期總成績未達60分者，不得續修下學期。

AA-CP-04-CF08 (1.2 版)／101.11.15 修訂

#### OCR 153: files/COURSES/602CC/106CC-3.docx

- 關聯類型: 超連結（檔案）

- 本系必修課程，上學期總成績未達40分者，不得續修下學期。
For compulsory subjects of faculty, students must score 40 marks and above before joining the next semester.
